**【章节】Cardiovascular**

在标准心电图（纸速 25 mm/s）中，横轴代表时间，纵轴代表电压（振幅）。以下是具体的数值总结：

1️⃣ 横轴：代表时间 (Time)

> 一个小格（1 mm）：0.04 秒 (40 ms) 。
>
> 一个大格（5 个小格）：0.20 秒 (200 ms) 。

*记忆技巧*：5 个大格正好等于 1 秒。

2️⃣ 纵轴：代表电压 (Voltage)

> 一个小格（1 mm）：0.1 毫伏 (0.1 mV)。
>
> 一个大格（5 个小格）：0.5 毫伏 (0.5 mV)。

*记忆技巧*：两个大格（10 mm）代表 1 mV（这是标准定标电压）。

🧠 临床应用：快速看图法

利用这些格数，你可以迅速判断 Step 2 CK 中的核心指标：

> 计算心率（300法则）：

两个 R 波之间有 **2 个大格** → 心率是 \$300 ÷ 2 = **150 bpm（常提示 2:1 房扑）**。

两个 R 波之间有 3 个大格 → 心率是 \$300 ÷ 3 = 100 bpm。

> 判断 PR 间期：

正常 PR 间期为 3-5 个小格 (0.12-0.20 秒)。

如果 \< 3 个小格 → 提示预激（WPW）。

如果 \> 5 个小格 → 提示一度房室传导阻滞。

> 判断 QRS 宽度：

正常宽度 \< 3 个小格 (0.12 秒) 。

如果 ≥ 3 个小格 → 宽 QRS 波（如 VT 或 WPW 逆向型）。

老年患者，心室壁增厚但 EF 正常、伴双心房扩大及肾脏等多系统受累表现，应高度怀疑心肌**<u>淀粉样变性引起的限制性心肌病</u>**。

对于伴有左心室肥厚表现的年轻高血压患者，应通过四肢血压测量和肱-股动脉搏动对比来筛查**<u>主动脉缩窄</u>**。

对于初步诊断为间歇性跛行的 PAD 患者，在启动**阿司匹林**和**他汀**治疗后，下一步最佳管理方案是开始**<span class="mark">监督下的运动疗法</span>**。

对于 CHA_2DS_2-VASc评分≥2的**房颤**患者，应首选**口服抗凝药（如 Apixaban）**来预防包括急性肢体缺血在内的全身栓塞事件 。房颤🡪PAD

如果患者有**中重度二尖瓣狭窄**或**机械瓣膜**，则必须使用**华法林**，不能使用 DOAC。

在**高血压**的生活方式干预中，**DASH 饮食**是降低收缩压最有效的单项措施，平均可使血压下降 11 mm Hg。

**持续性室速**：

稳定：首选<span class="mark">药物复律（静脉胺碘酮）</span>。

有脉但不稳定：立即同步电复律 。

无脉搏：按室颤处理（非同步电除颤）。

长期管理：**<span class="mark">EF ≤35% 且有持续性 VT</span>🡪<span class="mark">ICD植入</span>**；**beta-blocker, amiodarone, 导管消融**

**阵发性室速\<30s：**

**<span class="mark">纠正诱因：补钾、补镁</span> 。**

**2. 优化基础药：首选 <span class="mark">β-受体阻滞剂</span> 。**

**3. 禁用：I 类抗心律失常药**

看到**心衰**病人**呼吸困难加重**，如果**利尿剂无效**且**不烧**，眼睛一定要扫描药物清单里的 **<u>Amiodarone</u>**！

**IE 患者若伴有新发的心脏传导阻滞和主动脉瓣反流杂音，应立即通过 <span class="mark">TEE</span> 排除<span class="mark">瓣周脓肿</span>**

**<span class="mark">IE + 心跳慢/传导阻滞 = 脓肿</span>**

对于突发突止的规整窄 QRS 波心动过速（PSVT），迷走神经刺激通过**降低房室结（AV node）的传导**性来打破折返环。虽然迷走神经也会降低窦房结（SA node）的自律性，但终止 AVNRT 的关键在于打破房室结内的折返，而非改变窦房结的频率。

对于出现**劳力性气短、脉压差增大且在左侧卧位有明显心脏重击感**的**年轻**患者，应首先考虑**<u>慢性主动脉瓣反流</u>**。看到 **<span class="mark">150/45mmHg</span>**这种极端的血压，不用看别的，直接搜索 Aortic Regurgitation！**左侧卧位重击感**是它的独门特征。

**无论是阵发性、持续性还是永久性<span class="mark">房颤</span>，其导致系统性栓塞（如卒中）的风险是相似的** 。无论房颤是否已转复，<span class="mark">只要**CHA_2DS_2-VASc评分达标**，就应启动**长期抗凝治疗**</span>**（首选 DOACs）**。若患者有**中重度二尖瓣狭窄或机械瓣膜**，则必须使用**华法林**

伴有广泛动脉粥样硬化表现的**顽固性高血压**患者，应高度怀疑**<u>肾动脉狭窄renovascular hypertension</u>**，腹部持续性杂音是其特征性体征

**CCB引起的外周水肿源于毛细血管静水压增高，首选联合使用<span class="mark">CCB+ ACEI 或 ARB</span> 扩张小静脉**🡪**缓解外周水肿症状并强化降压效果**

**digoxin** 增强迷走作用🡪**减慢 AV 结传导**；同时有**轻度正性肌力**作用，所以在 **<span class="mark">AF + HFrEF</span>** 时可以用，**尤其当<u>血压偏低</u>**<u>, **beta blocker / CCB 不合适**</u>, 或作为联合用药。中毒：**<span class="mark">恶心 + 黄绿视 + 房速+AV block</span>**

**对于目击下的院外心脏骤停，最常为VT/VF🡪rhythm analysis and defibrillation，<span class="mark">电除颤</span>时间是决定患者生存的最重要因素**

**无脉性房颤属于PEA, 通常由于严重的机械性问题（如大面积肺栓塞、张力性气胸、严重低血容量）导致心脏虽有电信号但无射血功能**

对于表现为无脉性电活动（PEA）的心脏骤停患者，应立即启动高质量胸外按压（CPR），并在复苏过程中积极寻找并纠正 **5H & 5T 可逆因素** 。

急性心包炎是总称 ；**PIP** 是 MI 后 **1–4 天**的局部炎症 ；**PCIS** 是心脏损伤（手术、外伤、PCI）数周后的免疫性心包炎 ；**Dressler** 则是 MI 引发的特定 PCIS 。

**典型表现**：**体位性胸痛（坐起减轻 ）、向肩部放射** 、心包摩擦音 及 ECG **弥漫性 PR 段压低与 ST 段抬高 。**

**首选检查**：无论何种亚型，<span class="mark">新发胸痛首选 **Echo**</span> 以排除心包填塞或心脏游离壁破裂 。

**PIP 治疗红线**：心梗后早期（**\<4天**）**严禁使用 NSAIDs 或激素**（增加破裂风险 ），支持治疗，首选**<span class="mark">Acetaminophen</span>**镇痛 。

**PCIS/Dressler 治疗**：心梗或损伤数周后发病 ，首选**<span class="mark">大剂量阿司匹林 + 秋水仙碱</span>** 。

**Dressler 特殊风险**：处理 Dressler 综合征时需**暂停或小心抗凝药**，防止诱发出血性心包积液 。

**尿毒症性心包炎**：常见于 **BUN \>60** mg/dL 患者 ，特征是 **ECG 通常无 ST/PR 改变** ，首选治疗为**<span class="mark">血液透析</span>** 。

**SLE 相关心包炎**：多见于 SLE 活动期 ，首选 **<span class="mark">NSAIDs</span>** ；若合并肾功不全则改用**<span class="mark">皮质类固醇</span>** 。

**劳力性晕厥**在**老年人**中首选排除**严重主动脉瓣狭窄（看颈动脉搏动）**，在**青年人**中首选排除**肥厚型心肌病（做 Valsalva 试验）**，而有**心脏病史**者需警惕**室速**发作。**首选检查：<span class="mark">Echo看结构</span>**，然后**ECG, 生化/电解质**。

快速心律失常

**血流动力学不稳定**（低血压/休克/急性心衰）：不看心律，直接 **同步电复律** 。

**血流动力学稳定**：

**窄 QRS**：**迷走神经动作 🡪 IV Adenosine**

> **转复后**：所有窄波复律后必查静息 ECG，寻找 **Delta 波**🡪**WPW**, 根治选 **导管消融**

**宽 QRS**：禁用 ABCD，首选 **Procainamide**

**Cocaine-associated chest pain🡪IV benzodiazepines; 其它：aspirin, nitroglycerin, CCB**

稳定性缺血性心脏病（SIHD），患者必须启动二级预防治疗🡪↓MI risk

Antiplatelet (aspirin)

High-intensity statin (atorvastatin, rosuvastatin)

风险控制：降压、控糖、戒烟、运动。

**Smoking cessation** is 1<sup>st</sup> line intervention for **peripheral artery disease**

**Leg elevation, leg exercises, compression** for **chronic venous insufficiency**

**Stable, asymptomatic patient with adequate functional capacity can proceed to noncardiac surgery without further cardiac testing.**

| 题干线索 | 答案方向 |
|:---|:---|
| Emergency surgery | Proceed to surgery |
| Unstable angina/recent MI/decompensated HF/severe valve disease | Postpone surgery, treat cardiac condition |
| Low-risk surgery | No further cardiac testing |
| RCRI 0–1 | Proceed to surgery |
| RCRI ≥2 + functional capacity ≥4 METs | Proceed to surgery |
| RCRI ≥2 + \<4 METs + testing changes management | Pharmacologic stress test |
| Old MI on ECG but asymptomatic and good METs | No further testing |
| New murmur/syncope/dyspnea/orthopnea/edema | Echocardiography |
| Hemodynamically unstable AF | Electrical cardioversion |
| Stable AF with rapid rate | Rate control first |

**Heart Sounds, Murmur Clues, and Lead Localization**

**Heart Sounds**

**S1**

> **Closure** of the **mitral and tricuspid valves**
>
> First heart sound

**S2**

> Closure of the **aortic and pulmonic valves**

**S3**

> Associated with a **dilated heart**
>
> Seen in dilated cardiomyopathy
>
> Can be **normal** in:

**<span class="mark">Pregnancy</span>**

**<span class="mark">Right before menses</span>**

**S4**

> Associated with a **hypertrophied, stiff ventricle**
>
> Seen with **longstanding hypertension** and other causes of **ventricular hypertrophy**
>
> **Never normal**

**Murmur Sound Clues**

**<span class="mark">Loud S2</span>**

> **Aortic stenosis**
>
> **Pulmonic stenosis**

**<span class="mark">Soft S1</span>**

> **Mitral regurgitation**
>
> **Tricuspid regurgitation**

**Murmur Radiation aortic valve🡪carotids; pulmonic valve🡪back; mitral valve🡪axilla**

**To the carotids**

> <span class="mark">Aortic</span> stenosis
>
> Aortic regurgitation

**To the back**

> <span class="mark">Pulmonic</span> stenosis
>
> Pulmonic regurgitation

**To the axilla**

> <span class="mark">Mitral</span> regurgitation
>
> Mitral stenosis

**Maneuvers 背**

**<span class="mark">Standing / Valsalva makes louder</span> (静脉回流减少🡪左室充盈减少/preload↓🡪左室腔变小)**

> **Mitral valve prolapse** （瓣膜更早脱垂）
>
> **HOCM**

**<span class="mark">Handgrip makes softer</span> （外周血管阻力↑🡪afterload↑）**

> **HOCM** (afterload↑🡪左室排空↓🡪左室相对变大)
>
> **Mitral valve prolapse**
>
> **Aortic stenosis** （afterload↑🡪跨瓣压↓🡪流过的血量减少，流速变小）

**Squatting** (**preload ↑ + afterload ↑**🡪左室充盈↑🡪室腔变大)

> <span class="mark">HOCM, Mitral valve prolapse🡪softer</span>
>
> <span class="mark">Aortic stenosis🡪louder</span> （增加静脉回流和射血量🡪更多血通过瓣膜）**狭窄杂音主要看通过瓣膜的血流量**

**<span class="mark">Holosystic murmur</span>**

**MR: apex🡪axilla**

**TR:** 胸骨左缘1-2肋间，**<span class="mark">murmur ↑with inspiration三尖返流吸气响</span>**

**VSD**：**左缘3-4肋间, loudest at tricuspid area**

**<span class="mark">Mid-systolic click</span> + late systolic murmur**

**Mitral valve prolapse/MVP**

**脱垂（prolapse） 是 瓣叶形态/位置异常；\
返流（regurgitation） 是 功能异常，真的有血倒流。**

**吸气🡪右心杂音增强，呼气🡪左心杂音增强**

**Acute MR**🡪 sudden-onset large-volume backflow of blood from LV to LA.  **Neither chamber has time for compensatory dilation**🡪rapid ↑LV end-diastolic pressure and LA pressure🡪**pulmonary edema.** 

Although forward blood flow is reduced, left ventricular ejection fraction is normal or hyperdynamic.

**EKG Territory Basics**

<img src="images/media/image1.jpeg" style="width:2.8875in;height:2.98889in" />**Chamber / Lead Associations**

**Right atrium**

> V1
>
> aVR

**Left atrium**

> Lead I
>
> aVL
>
> V2 （靠近房间隔）

**Right ventricle**

> Lead II
>
> aVF

**Left ventricle**

> Lead III
>
> V3
>
> V5
>
> V6
>
> some aVF

**Coronary Supply Basics**

**Artery supplying most（85%）of the heart**

> **Left main** coronary artery

**Dominant artery**

> Usually the **right main** coronary artery
>
> Supplies the SA node and AV node

**Chest Pain Differential**

**<u>Pericarditis</u>**

**Presentation**

> Chest pain
>
> Better when **leaning forward 体位性胸痛**
>
> Worse lying back
>
> May have friction rub
>
> If patient **holds breath**, the friction rub **stays present**

**EKG**

> **<span class="mark">Diffuse ST elevation</span>**
>
> **PR depression** may also be seen
>
> Can have **low-voltage QRS**

**Dx:**

> **<span class="mark">Echocardiography</span>** **评估心包积液、心脏功能**
>
> Echo may show **thickened pericardium**

只有 ECG 改变 = **Acute Pericarditis**。

ECG 改变 + 心肌酶升高 (Troponin/CK-MB) = **Myopericarditis**。 这种情况需要更密切的监护，因为心肌炎症可能导致心律失常或暂时性的心室功能障碍

**Treatment🡪based on cause**

> **After infection**
>
> **<span class="mark">NSAIDs</span>**
>
> **Due to kidney failure / uremia**
>
> **<span class="mark">Dialysis</span>** (uremia building up irritating it)
>
> **After MI**
>
> **Dressler syndrome** (**fever** and **pleuritic chest pain,** Acute pericarditis occurring 2–3 weeks after MI)
>
> Treat with **<span class="mark">high-dose aspirin</span>**
>
> **Recurrent pericarditis:<span class="mark">Colchicine</span>**

**<u>Costochondritis</u>**

**Presentation**

> **Reproducible chest pain on exam**

**EKG (best initial)**

> **Normal**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">NSAIDs</span>**

**<u>Esophageal Spasm</u>**

**Presentation**

> **Substernal chest pain**
>
> <span class="mark">Triggered by **cold liquids**</span>
>
> **<span class="mark">Dysphagia</span>**

**Imaging**

**corkscrew**

**Most Accurate Test**

> **<span class="mark">Manometry</span>**
>
> Abnormal peristalsis
>
> ↑sphincter pressure

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Calcium channel blocker</span>**

**<u>Aortic Dissection</u>**

**Presentation**

> **Sharp or tearing chest pain** **radiating to the back** (疼痛升主动脉偏前胸，降主动脉偏背部)
>
> May have:

New diastolic murmur

**Asymmetric pulses** （分支血管灌注受损）

**Neurologic deficits** （颈动脉、脑血管或脊髓供血分支受累）

Horner syndrome **(unilateral ptosis, miosis, anhydrosis)（**夹层/血肿压迫颈部交感链）

**Blood Pressure Clue**

> **BP differs between <span class="mark">arms</span>**
>
> <span class="mark">**Ddx: Upper vs lower extremity difference** suggests **coarctation**</span>, not dissection

**Imaging**

**Chest x-ray**

> **<span class="mark">Widened mediastinum</span>**

**Most accurate**

> **CT angiography**

**<span class="mark">Unstable echo?</span>**

**Treatment**

**First step**

> <span class="mark">**Lower BP** with **beta blocker**</span> first
>
> Then **<span class="mark">sodium nitroprusside</span>** if needed

**Ascending dissection**

> Stabilize with **labetalol/nitroprusside**
>
> Then **<span class="mark">surgery</span>**

**Descending dissection**

> <span class="mark">**BP control** only</span> (**hydralazine, labetalol, carvedilol, sodium nitroprusside**)
>
> No surgery in most cases

<table style="width:95%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 19%" />
<col style="width: 75%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Acute aortic dissection</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Risk factors</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><mark>Chronic <strong>hypertension</strong></mark> (<strong>strongest</strong> overall risk factor)</p>
<p>Underlying aortopathy (eg, <strong>Marfan syndrome, Turner</strong>)</p>
<p><strong>Cocaine</strong> use</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical presentation</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Severe, tearing</strong> <strong>chest or back pain</strong>, maximal at onset</p>
<p>± Variation in SBP between arms &gt;20 mm Hg</p>
<p>Hypertension usually present*</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Diagnosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>ECG</mark></strong>: normal or nonspecific ST-segment &amp; T-wave changes</p>
<p><strong><mark>Chest x-ray</mark></strong>: mediastinal widening</p>
<p><strong><mark>CT angiography or TEE</mark></strong> for <strong>definitive diagnosis</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Pain control</mark> (eg, morphine)</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>IV beta blockers</mark> (eg, esmolol)</strong></p>
<p><strong>± <mark>Sodium nitroprusside</mark> (if SBP &gt;120 mm Hg despite beta blockers)</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Emergency surgical repair</mark> for ascending dissection</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">*Hypotension on presentation suggests aortic rupture or other complication (eg, cardiac tamponade, acute aortic regurgitation). <strong>SBP</strong> = systolic blood pressure; <strong>TEE</strong> = transesophageal echocardiography.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>Pneumothorax</u>**

**Presentation**

> **Young patient**
>
> **Sudden chest pain**
>
> **Shortness of breath**
>
> **Decreased breath sounds**, hyperresonance
>
> **<span class="mark">张力性气胸🡪JVD</span>** (高压空气压迫肺、纵膈、上腔静脉、心脏🡪静脉血回不到右心🡪obstructive shock)

**Best Initial Test**

> Chest x-ray

**X-ray Clues**

**Tension pneumothorax**

**Tracheal deviation away** from affected side

**Spontaneous pneumothorax**

**no tracheal deviation**

**Treatment Locations**

**<span class="mark">Needle decompression</span>**

> Between **2nd and 3rd ribs**
>
> **Midclavicular line**
>
> **Above** the rib

**<span class="mark">Chest tube</span>**

> **4th–5th intercostal space**
>
> **Midaxillary line**
>
> **Above** the rib

**<u>Hemothorax</u>**

**Presentation**

> Decreased breath sounds on one side
>
> Chest pain
>
> **<span class="mark">Flat neck veins</span>** / **no JVD** (失血🡪hypovolemic shock)

**Treatment**

> Chest tube (tube thoracostomy胸廓造口术)

**Escalate to <span class="mark">Surgery</span> If**

> Initial drainage **\>1000** mL
>
> Continued bleeding **150–200** mL **after 2–4 hours**
>
> Persistent hemodynamic **instability**

**<u>Cocaine-Induced Chest Pain</u>=chest pian + dilated pupils**

**Why It Causes Chest Pain**

> Increased **sympathetic activity🡪 <span class="mark">Dilated pupils</span>** are a clue
>
> Coronary vasospasm

**EKG**

> **<span class="mark">ST elevation</span>** can occur from **coronary artery spasm**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">MONA</span>** initially if needed急性冠脉综合征/心梗（ACS/MI）**初始处理**

**M=morphine**

**O=oxygen**

**N=nitroglycerin**

**A=aspirin**

> Try **<span class="mark">calcium channel blocker</span>** first
>
> **<span class="mark">Benzodiazepines</span>** (diazepam, lorazepam) also help🡪降低交感兴奋，减少心肌耗氧，用于cociane-induced ACS
>
> If **ST elevation persists**, go to **<span class="mark">cath lab / PCI</span>**

**If EKG is Normal**

> **Benzodiazepine**

**<span class="mark">cocaine chest pain → benzodiazepine + nitrates</span>, 不能用 β-blocker（会加重血管收缩）**

**【继续复习】**

**<u>Panic Attack</u>**

**Presentation不可预测**

> Chest pain
>
> Sweating
>
> **Tachycardia**
>
> SOB
>
> Often **situational,** such as just before a speech

**Exam / EKG**

> **EKG normal**
>
> Physical exam normal

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Benzodiazepine</span> (Alprazolam)**

**<u>Coronary Artery Disease and Angina</u>**

<table style="width:65%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 23%" />
<col style="width: 41%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">Pretest probability of coronary artery disease</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Low (&lt;10%)</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Asymptomatic people of all ages</p>
<p>Atypical chest pain in women age &lt;50</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Intermediate (20%-80%)</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Atypical angina in men of all ages</p>
<p>Atypical angina in women age ≥50</p>
<p>Typical angina in women age 30-50</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">High (&gt;90%)</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Typical angina in men age ≥40</p>
<p>Typical angina in women age ≥60</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<table style="width:65%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 11%" />
<col style="width: 53%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">Classification of angina</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Classic</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Typical location (eg, substernal), quality &amp; duration</p>
<p>Provoked by exercise or emotional stress</p>
<p>Relieved by rest or nitroglycerin</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Atypical</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>2 of the 3 characteristics of classic angina</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Nonanginal</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>&lt;2 of the 3 characteristics of classic angina</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>Evaluation of chest pain</u>**

<img src="images/media/image2.jpeg" style="width:5.06962in;height:4.06206in" />

**CAD Risk Factors**

**Greatest risk factor**

> **<span class="mark">Diabetes</span>**--preventable

**Most preventable**

> Smoking

**<u>Stable Angina</u>**

**Presentation**

> Exertional chest pain
>
> Relieved by rest
>
> Usually due to **atherosclerosis with about 70% stenosis**

**稳定型心绞痛的“变体”**

> **典型稳定型心绞痛： 运动诱发，休息 5-10 分钟缓解。**
>
> **不典型心绞痛（多见于<span class="mark">女性/糖尿病</span>）： 表现为<span class="mark">气短、烧心、背痛、腹痛</span>，诱因<span class="mark">仍是劳力性</span>。**
>
> **<span class="mark">平卧位心绞痛 (Angina Decubitus)</span>： 发生在躺下时，因为回心血量增加了心脏负担。**

**如果一个糖尿病人告诉你，她干活的时候“胃疼”，休息一下就好点，但晚上躺着还是有点难受，千万不要只给她开胃药。在手术前，一定要先用压力测试（Stress Test）确认她的血管还是通的。**

**<span class="mark">EKG</span>**

> **<span class="mark">Normal at rest</span>**

**Next Step**

> **<span class="mark">Stress test</span> <span class="mark">Max Heart Rate=</span>**<span class="mark">220 – age</span>, above that🡪arrythmia

**Stress Test Selection**

**Cannot exercise / uses walker**

> <span class="mark">**Dipyridamole**/**adenosine**</span>（扩张正常冠脉，病变血管不能扩张🡪出现coronary steal🡪显示缺血）

**COPD / asthma**

> **<span class="mark">Dobutamine</span> stress echo** （β1 agonist🡪↑ HR + contractility）
>
> **dipyridamole / adenosine**会↑ adenosine→ **bronchospasm**

**Pacemaker**

> **<span class="mark">Thallium</span> stress test** （Thallium /铊像 potassium，能进活心肌，**直接看灌注**；Pacemaker 会造成**ECG 不可靠，**ST segment 无法解读，所以**不能用 ECG-based stress test）**

**Left bundle branch block**

> **<span class="mark">Thallium</span> stress test**（LBBB 会导致左室激动延迟，septal motion 异常，ECG ST-T 改变，即使没有缺血也可能出现**假阳性（false positive）**）

**If Stress Test Is Abnormal**

> **<span class="mark">Cath lab / PCI</span>**

<img src="images/media/image3.png" style="width:4.97857in;height:1.35823in" />

| 场景 | 推荐组合 | 理由 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 能运动 + 静息ECG正常 | 运动 + ECG | 最简单、最便宜。 |
| 能运动 + **静息ECG异常** | 运动 + **影像 (超声或核素)** | ECG已经乱了，必须用影像直接看肉或看血。 |
| **不能运动** (肥胖/残疾) | **药物** + 影像 (超声或核素) | 药物压力测试，必须配合影像才能评估。 |

** 压力手段 (Stressors)：**

> 运动压力： 跑步机（Treadmill）。
>
> 药物压力： 针对不能运动的患者，用药物模拟运动。

多巴酚丁胺 (Dobutamine)：增加心率和收缩力。

腺苷 (Adenosine) / 嘧啶达莫 (Dipyridamole)：扩张血管，产生“窃血现象”。

** 监测/显像工具 (Imaging)：**

> 心电图 (ECG)：最基础，看电信号。
>
> 超声 (Echocardiography)：看解剖结构和运动。
>
> 核素 (Nuclear/Scintigraphy)：看血流灌注。

**Stable angina → outpatient stress test\
Unstable angina → hospital admission**

**<u>Prinzmetal Angina</u>**

**Presentation**

> **Coronary vasospasm**
>
> Episodic chest pain
>
> Not related to physical activity
>
> Often **severe and brief**
>
> Risk factor: smoking

**EKG**

> Transient ST elevation during spasm

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Calcium channel blockers</span>**

**稳定性缺血性心脏病（SIHD），患者必须启动二级预防治疗🡪↓MI risk**

**Antiplatelet (aspirin)**

**High-intensity statin (atorvastatin, rosuvastatin)**

**风险控制：降压、控糖、戒烟、运动。**

**<u>CABG Indications</u>三支病、糖尿病、左主干**

> 3-vessel disease
>
> 2-vessel disease with **diabetes**
>
> Proximal **LAD \>70%** occluded (供血前壁+室间隔🡪widow maker)
>
> Low EF<span class="mark">\<35%</span>
>
> Medical therapy failed

**<u>Myocardial Infarction</u>**

**Classic Presentation**

> Older patient
>
> Chest pain
>
> Sweating
>
> **Pain radiating to <span class="mark">jaw</span>**

**Atypical Presentation**

<img src="images/media/image4.png" style="width:3.61806in;height:3.39167in" />In:

> **<span class="mark">Diabetics</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Women</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Elderly</span>**

May present with:

> **<span class="mark">Sudden flu-like symptoms, no pain</span>**

**Initial Management**

**<u>Best initial step</u>**

> **<span class="mark">MONA</span>** while hooking patient to **<span class="mark">EKG</span>**

**<span class="mark">MONA</span>**

> Morphine🡪减轻疼痛和交感兴奋🡪间接减少耗氧
>
> Oxygen
>
> Nitroglycerin🡪心肌耗氧↓，部分改善冠脉灌注
>
> **SBP\<100 (right-sided involvement) DON’T USE**
>
> Aspirin**<span class="mark">抗板</span>**🡪血栓↓
>
> Sometimes beta blocker
>
> <img src="images/media/image5.png" style="width:4.37388in;height:1.26856in" />

**When Not to Give Nitrates**

> <span class="mark">Systolic BP ≤100</span>
>
> Think about possible **right-sided involvement**

<img src="images/media/image6.png" style="width:3.89167in;height:4.36181in" />**ST Depression Differential**

> **Unstable angina**
>
> **NSTEMI**

**Next Step <u>After MONA + Abnormal EKG</u>**

> **<span class="mark">Heparin抗凝</span>**
>
> Then <span class="mark">cardiac enzymes</span>

**Which One Has Positive Enzymes?**

> **NSTEMI**

**If Enzymes Are Positive**

> **<span class="mark">Cath lab\<90 min</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">tPA if delayed</span>**

**<u>ST Elevation MI</u>**

**Next Step**

**<span class="mark">PCI</span>** if door-to-cath time **\<90 min**

**If major delay**

> **<span class="mark">tPA</span>** first**<span class="mark">溶栓</span>**
>
> Then **<span class="mark">cath lab</span>**

**<span class="mark">MI处理无CTA！！！</span>That’s for PE!**

<table style="width:92%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 22%" />
<col style="width: 69%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">Management of <strong>ST-segment elevation myocardial infarction</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Nitrates</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Caution</strong> with <strong>hypotension (eg, RV infarction)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Beta blockers</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Oral cardioselective (eg, metoprolol, atenolol)</p>
<p><strong>Contraindicated</strong> in <strong>heart failure &amp; bradycardia (负时负力)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Antiplatelet therapy</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Aspirin &amp; P2Y<sub>12</sub></strong> receptor blocker (eg, <strong>ticagrelor</strong>)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Anticoagulation</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Unfractionated heparin, enoxaparin, or bivalirudin</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Statin therapy</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>High potency (eg, atorvastatin, rosuvastatin)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Coronary reperfusion</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>PCI ≤90 min</strong> from first medical contact</p>
<p><strong>Fibrinolytics (eg, alteplase)</strong> if PCI is unavailable</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

STEMI + acute pulmonary edema🡪furosemide±IV nitrates，根本治疗PCI

NDH-CCB负性肌力，加重肺水肿，急性MI不用

**<u>High risk pt or ongoing ACS symptoms in emergency</u>**

**<span class="mark">Serial ECG</span>, 15-30min intervals + <span class="mark">serial cardiac biomarkers</span>**

**If normal🡪<span class="mark">bedside echocardiography</span>**

**After ACS/acute symptoms🡪<span class="mark">stress test</span>**

<img src="images/media/image7.png" style="width:4.09326in;height:2.9958in" />

**<u>MI Localization</u>**

**Inferior MI**

> Leads <span class="mark">II, III, aVF</span>
>
> <span class="mark">RCA</span>

**Anterior MI🡪most deadly**

> V1, V2, V3, V4
>
> Especially **<span class="mark">V3 and V4</span>**
>
> <span class="mark">LAD</span>

**Posterior MI**

> PDA
>
> <img src="images/media/image1.jpeg" style="width:2.26806in;height:2.34792in" />Can see:

V1–V3 ST depression

V7–V9 elevation

**High Lateral MI**

> Lead I，aVL
>
> V2 as noted in these notes
>
> Left main distribution conceptually
>
> <img src="images/media/image8.png" style="width:3.55208in;height:1.21736in" />

**Septal Infarct**

> **Q waves in V1 and V2**
>
> Can be “**silent infarcts**”

**Cardiac Enzymes in Order of Peak**

> Myoglobin (within 2h)
>
> Troponin (within 4-6h)
>
> CK-MB (within 4-6h)
>
> AST—also find in heart
>
> LDH (48-72h)

**CK-MB**

> Rises and falls within about 24 hours
>
> Useful for detecting **reinfarction**

<img src="images/media/image9.png" style="width:3.84957in;height:1.30003in" />

**<u>MI Complications</u>**

**1st**

> Another MI

**Helps diagnose <span class="mark">reinfarction</span>**

> **<span class="mark">CK-MB</span>**

**2nd**

> **Ventricular arrhythmia**
>
> **Most deadly** early complication

**3<sup>rd</sup>—structural complications**

> **Papillary muscle rupture** → regurgitation
>
> **Ventricular septal rupture** → VSD
>
> **Free wall rupture** → tamponade or death

**Late complications:**

> **4th**
>
> **Aneurysm**
>
> **5th**
>
> **Dressler syndrome**

Presents like pericarditis weeks later

Treat with <span class="mark">high dose **aspirin**</span>

**<u>Perioperative MI</u>**

**noncardiac surgery, intraoperative hemorrhage requiring blood transfusion** increases the risk (likely due to reduced oxygen delivery to the myocardium)

**<span class="mark">lack chest pain</span>**, possibly due to receipt of postoperative pain control (eg, morphine)

**LV infarction**🡪LV impaired systolic dysfunction 🡪**LA pressure/PCWP↑, pulmonary edema, cardiogenic shock**

**Bradycardia, Blocks, and Arrhythmias**

**<u>Bradycardia</u>**

**Presentation**

> Often older patient
>
> HR \<60
>
> Syncope
>
> SOB
>
> Can be asymptomatic

**Treatment**

> **Atropine（抗M2，升心律&contractility）**
>
> **Pacemaker**

**Complications**

> Clot causing stroke or MI

**<u>First-Degree Heart Block</u>**

**EKG**

> **Prolonged PR** (\>200msec, 5个小格，1个大格)

**Clinical Clues**

> Usually **asymptomatic**
>
> Tends to go away with **<span class="mark">exercise</span>**

**Infectious Causes：**Mnemonic: **<span class="mark">LSD loves company</span>**

> **Legionella**
>
> **Salmonella**
>
> **Diphtheria**
>
> **Lyme**
>
> **Chagas**

**Drugs Contraindicated in Heart Blocks**

> **Beta blockers**
>
> **Calcium channel blockers**

<img src="images/media/image10.png" style="width:3.92014in;height:1.66458in" />**<u>Second-Degree Mobitz I</u>**

**EKG: <span class="mark">progressive PR🡪drop</span>**

> **Progressive** PR prolongation
>
> Then dropped QRS

**Clinical**

> **Symptomatic** in these notes
>
> **<span class="mark">Exercise</span> and monitor**

<img src="images/media/image11.png" style="width:3.93542in;height:1.51528in" />**<u>Second-Degree Mobitz II</u>**

**EKG: <span class="mark">random drop</span>**

> **PR interval normal**
>
> **QRS drops erratically**

**Symptoms**

> Lightheadedness
>
> Syncope
>
> Dizziness

**Treatment <span class="mark">drug before pacemaker</span>**

> **<span class="mark">Atropine</span>** first
>
> **Pacemaker**

**<u>Third-Degree Heart Block</u>**

**EKG: <span class="mark">AV dissociation</span>**

> P waves and QRS complexes present
>
> **No relationship** between them

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Atropine</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Pacemaker</span>**

**<span class="mark">Fever + Normal HR Clue</span>**

If patient has fever but heart rate does not appropriately rise:

> Think **heart block**
>
> Or **heavy beta blocker use**

**Heart Sound Mentioned**

> <span class="mark">S3</span> (heart block合并心衰)

**<span class="mark">Cannon a waves</span>**=**心房收缩时，三尖瓣刚好关闭**，导致**颈静脉巨大 a 波**

常见于：

**Complete heart block**

Ventricular tachycardia

Junctional rhythm / junctional tachycardia

PVCs 之后偶发

**Atrial Arrhythmias**

**<u>Atrial Fibrillation</u>**

发生率随**年纪**增加而显著增加，与**atrial enlargement**🡪atrial remodeling相关

**Presentation**

> Palpitations
>
> Fluttering
>
> **Weakness**
>
> **Funny feeling in chest**

血栓风险↑

伴心室率增加时🡪CO↓

早期**paroxysmal/intermittent**🡪后期persistent/permanent

<img src="images/media/image12.png" style="width:4.58681in;height:0.91111in" />**EKG / Pulse**

> **No P waves**
>
> **Irregularly irregular** pulse
>
> (atria begin to experience rapid, asynchronous depolariztions)

**If EKG is Normal but Suspicion Remains**

> **<span class="mark">Holter monitor / observation</span>**

**<span class="mark"><u>Rate Control</u></span>** 【**rate under control before rhythm, rate is atrium, rhythm is ventricle**】

**No prior heart disease**

**<span class="mark">Calcium channel blocker</span>** (depolarize atrium) **most common**

这里指的是无明显结构性心脏病/无收缩性心衰 的 AF 病人，常用 非二氢吡啶类 CCB：**diltiazem 或 verapamil** 做 rate control。它们通过**减慢 AV 结传导**，让心室率降下来。

**<span class="mark">Longstanding HTN</span>, hear <span class="mark">S4</span>** (more time to fill)

**<span class="mark">Beta blocker</span>**

如果病人长期高血压、听到 S4，常提示 左室肥厚/舒张功能差/心脏偏硬。这类病人常<u>合并**高交感状态**或高血压</u>，beta blocker 很常用，**既能减慢心率，又能降低心肌耗氧和血压**。

**<span class="mark">Dilated heart</span> / hear <span class="mark">S3</span>**

**<span class="mark">Digoxin</span>**

digoxin 增强迷走作用，**减慢 AV 结传导**；同时有**轻度正性肌力**作用，所以在 **<span class="mark">AF + HFrEF</span>** 时可以用，**尤其当<u>血压偏低</u>**<u>, **beta blocker / CCB 不合适**</u>, 或作为联合用药

**Order of Management**

> **Control rate first**
>
> **Then rhythm**

**<span class="mark">Anticoagulation</span>**

> Warfarin
>
> Aspirin
>
> Apixaban

**Warfarin vs Aspirin**

> **Comorbidities → warfarin**
>
> No comorbidities → aspirin

**Why Bridge Warfarin with Heparin?**

> Warfarin knocks out protein C and S first
>
> Temporary hypercoagulable state
>
> Bridge about **3 days**

**<span class="mark"><u>Rhythm Control</u></span>**

> **Sodium channel blocker**
>
> **Or cardioversion/shock**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 31%" />
<col style="width: 68%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Conditions that increase the risk of atrial fibrillation</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Precipitants of <mark>atrial dilation</mark> &amp;/or<br />
conduction remodeling</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Advanced age</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Systemic hypertension</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Mitral valve dysfunction</strong></p>
<p><strong>Left ventricular failure</strong></p>
<p><strong>Coronary artery disease &amp; related factors (eg, DM, smoking)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Obesity &amp; obstructive sleep apnea</strong> (OSA → intermittent hypoxia + negative intrathoracic pressure → left atrial remodeling/fibrosis + autonomic instability → AF)</p>
<p><strong>Chronic hypoxic lung disease (eg, COPD)</strong> （低氧/高碳酸血症 + 炎症纤维化 + 交感兴奋 + 胸腔压波动 + 肺高压致右房重构 → AF）</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Triggers of increased automaticity</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Hyperthyroidism</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Excessive <mark>alcohol use</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Increased sympathetic tone</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Acute illness (eg, <mark>sepsis, PE, MI)</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Cardiac surgery</mark></strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Sympathomimetic drugs (eg, <mark>cocaine</mark>)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

important risk factors:

**<span class="mark">Advanced age</span>**

Comorbidities🡪**<span class="mark">atrial dilation</span> (esp HTN, mitral valve disease, HF**)🡪atrial remodeling

**young patient + new onset AF**🡪**<span class="mark">check serum TSH level</span>**🡪evaluate **<span class="mark">hyperthyroidism</span>**

AF may be the only manifestation of hyperthyroidism

<img src="images/media/image13.png" style="width:5.09718in;height:1.80644in" />

**<u>Atrial fibrillation with rapid ventricular response</u>**（房颤伴快速**心室率(\>100)**，AF with RVR）

A fib🡪心悸, 胸口 fluttering, 气短, 乏力, 头晕, **血栓风险**

心室率太快🡪CO↓🡪低血压，胸痛，心衰加重🡪**肺水肿**

**Atrial fibrillation** is common **<span class="mark">following cardiac surgery</span>** (**coronary artery bypass grafting**, **aortic valve replacement**)

When a cardiac rhythm with such a highly rapid rate, acute management is determined by the **<span class="mark">hemodynamic stability</span>**

hemodynamically **<span class="mark">unstable</span>**🡪**<span class="mark">synchronized cardioversion</span>**

**Alcohol🡪A fib🡪ARDS (no anticoag needed)**

**** binge alcohol + new AF → 先想 **<span class="mark"><u>holiday heart syndrome</u></span>**

 处理重点是：

> 停酒：病因治疗
>
> 评估 hemodynamics

**不稳定**（低血压、急性心衰、严重胸痛）：立即**同步电复律**（Synchronized Cardioversion）。

**稳定**：首选**药物控率**（如 Beta-blockers 或 CCB）

> 控制心率/必要时复律

对于**假日心脏综合征**，由于它是**自限性**的，通常**控率（Rate Control）优先**。

如果 48 小时后仍未自行转复，再考虑药物或电复律

> 抗凝按 CHA₂DS₂-VASc 决定，不按“是不是酒精导致”决定

**<span class="mark">短期抗凝（复律期间）</span>：** 如果房颤发作持续超过 48 小时，或者时长不明，复律前必须按标准流程抗凝（或 TEE 排除血栓）。

<span class="mark">**长期抗凝：** 严格计算 **CHA₂DS₂-VASc 评分**</span>。

**CHA2DS2-VASc Score**

<img src="images/media/image14.png" style="width:3.00556in;height:2.68125in" />Used to estimate **embolic stroke (eg intracranial hemorrhage** **) risk**/ **thromboembolic risk** in **Afib/A flutter** 🡪是否需要长期抗凝

> CHF = 1
>
> HTN = 1
>
> Age \>75 = 2
>
> Diabetes = 1
>
> Stroke/TIA/thromboembolism = 2
>
> Vascular disease = 1
>
> Age 65–74 = 1
>
> Female sex = 1

<img src="images/media/image15.png" style="width:4.18958in;height:0.66389in" />≥2 risk high🡪oral anticoagulant (首选apixaban)

CHA_2DS_2-VASc评分表用于评估<span class="mark">**非瓣膜性房颤**患者的血栓风险并指导抗凝治疗</span> 。

| **字母** | **代表含义 (Risk Criteria)** | **分值 (Points)** | **记忆逻辑** |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| **C** | **C**ongestive heart failure (**心力衰竭**) | **1** | 心功能不全导致血流淤滞 。 |
| **H** | **H**ypertension (**高血压**) | **1** | 即使控制良好的高血压也算 。 |
| **A₂** | <span class="mark">**A**ge ≥ 75 (高龄)</span> | **<span class="mark">2</span>** | **"2"代表2分**，高龄是极高危因素 。 |
| **D** | **D**iabetes mellitus (**糖尿病**) | **1** | 代谢异常增加血栓风险 。 |
| **S₂** | <span class="mark">**S**troke / TIA / Thromboembolism (脑卒中史)</span> | **<span class="mark">2</span>** | **"2"代表2分**，既往史最重要 。 |
| **V** | **V**ascular disease (**血管疾病**) | **1** | 如陈旧心梗、外周动脉疾病 (PAD) 。 |
| **A** | **A**ge **65**-74 (中年以上) | **1** | 相比75岁，这个年龄段风险稍低 。 |
| **Sc** | **S**ex **c**ategory (性别) | **1** | **女性**增加1分风险 。 |

在整个表格中，只有两个因素是 **2分**，其余全是 **1分** ：

> **Age ≥ 75** (高龄) 。
>
> **Stroke / TIA** (卒中史) 。

**记忆逻辑**：年龄足够大和已经发生过中风的人，风险是最高的，所以给2分 。

| **性别** | **0 分** | **1 分** | **<span class="mark">≥ 2 分</span>** |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| **男性** | 无需抗凝 | 考虑抗凝或不抗凝 | **必须抗凝 (Oral Anticoagulant)** |
| **女性** | (由于性别自带1分，女性0分不存在) | 1 分（仅性别）：无需抗凝 | 2分：考虑抗凝；**≥ 3分：必须抗凝** |

**💡 考试避坑准则：**

> **阿司匹林不再推荐**：在房颤抗凝指南中，阿司匹林（抗血小板）已经基本退出舞台。如果评分达标，直接选<span class="mark">**口服抗凝药**（Warfarin 或 NOACs 如 Apixaban</span>） 。
>
> **性别陷阱**：女性只有在伴有**至少一个其他风险因素**时，性别分才会计入治疗考量 。
>
> 如果患者有<span class="mark">**中重度二尖瓣狭窄**或**人工机械瓣膜**</span> ：

**忽略 \$CHA_2DS_2-VASc\$ 评分** 。

**必须使用<span class="mark">华法林 (Warfarin)</span>** 进行抗凝（不能用新型抗凝药 NOACs） 。

房颤时心房失去有效收缩，血液在心耳瘀滞易形成血栓 。**无论是阵发性、持续性还是永久性房颤，其导致系统性栓塞（如卒中）的风险是相似的** 。无论房颤是否已转复，只要CHA_2DS_2-VASc评分达标，就应启动**长期抗凝治疗（首选 DOACs）**。若患者有**中重度二尖瓣狭窄或机械瓣膜**，则必须使用**华法林**

**<u>Atrial Flutter</u>**

**EKG**

> **Sawtooth** pattern
>
> Best seen in **II, III, aVF**

**Treatment**

> Similar to AFib
>
> **Calcium channel blocker** for **rate control**

**<u>Multifocal Atrial Tachycardia</u>**

**Who Gets It?**

> **<span class="mark">Long history of COPD</span>**
>
> <img src="images/media/image16.png" style="width:1.55486in;height:2.09167in" />Hypokalemia
>
> Sepsis (低K+, 低Mg2+)，hypoxia, 严重肺病

**Presentation**

> **Palpitations**
>
> **Weakness**
>
> **Funny feeling in chest**

**EKG** **= irregularly irregular tachycardia + ≥3种P波形态 + atrial rate \>100(乱而有P，P还长得不一样)**

> **Multiple P waves**
>
> Irregular narrowed-complex tachycardia, variable PR interval<img src="images/media/image17.png" style="width:4.59846in;height:1.51972in" />

**Treatment继发于肺病/低氧/应激的房性节律紊乱🡪先治病因，节律常自己好**

> **Oxygen**
>
> **Calcium channel blocker**
>
> Check electrolytes, especially **potassium**

**Distinction**

**<u>Wandering atrial pacemaker</u>游走性心房起搏点（起搏点不是固定在窦房结，而是在心房里“到处游走”，所以会出现多种不同形态的 P waves，但心率 \<100/min），良性，多见于儿童、老年人，有时和迷走神经张力变化有关，一般不严重**

> Multiple P waves too
>
> But **heart rate \<100**

<img src="images/media/image18.png" style="width:4.19851in;height:1.18939in" />

**Premature atrial complexes**

Benign arrhythmia

precipitating factors：**tobacco, alcohol, caffeine, and stress** should be identified andavoided

beta blockers for symptomatic pts

<img src="images/media/image19.png" style="width:4.34431in;height:1.23595in" />

**Ventricular Arrhythmias**

**<u>Ventricular Tachycardia</u>**

<img src="images/media/image20.jpeg" style="width:3.5125in;height:1.09444in" />**Presentation**

> **Tachycardia**
>
> **<span class="mark">Chest pain</span> vs atrial arrythmia don’t have chest pain**
>
> **Palpitations**
>
> Patient may **still be talking**

<img src="images/media/image21.png" style="width:5.26042in;height:0.92014in" />**EKG**

> Wide QRS
>
> “Mountains”

**Treatment**

**<span class="mark">Stable</span>**

> **Sodium channel blocker** (**<span class="mark">lidocaine</span>** IB)
>
> **Magnesium sulfate** can help shut down V tach, 用于**torsade**
>
> **Amiodarone** (III) may also be used

**<span class="mark">Unstable with pulse</span>**

> **<span class="mark">Synchronized cardioversion</span>🡪必须有QRS/pulse (unstable A Fib, A flutter, artrial tachy, SVT)**

**<span class="mark">No pulse</span>**

**<span class="mark">Defibrillation + CPR</span>**

**If patient doing ok then went unresponsive and <span class="mark">lost pulse （pulseless VT/VF）</span>**

> **<span class="mark">Unsynchronized cardioversion=Defibrillate</span>**

**有脉但不稳定🡪 synchronized cardioversion（不用CPR胸外按压）**

**无脉（pulseless VT/VF）🡪 defibrillate 🡪 CPR + epi 🡪抗心律失常药（amiodarone / lidocaine）**

**PEA/asystole🡪 CPR + epi**

**Epi ：alpha1🡪血管收缩，↑冠脉灌注**

<img src="images/media/image22.png" style="width:2.92639in;height:3.09583in" />

**<u>Ventricular Fibrillation</u>**

**Presentation**

> Often **VT 🡪 VF**
>
> Patient collapses (dropped to ground)

**EKG**

> No pulse
>
> Undulating chaotic line

**Treatment**

> **Defibrillation**
>
> **CPR**

**<u>PEA <span class="mark">pulseless electrical activity</span> / <span class="mark">Electrical Alternans</span> </u>**

**Presentation**心电图有组织的心律（如窦性、房颤、心动过缓），但无脉搏🡪无机械泵血🡪cardiac arrest

**通常由于严重的机械性问题（如大面积肺栓塞、张力性气胸、严重低血容量）导致心脏虽有电信号但无射血功能**

> No pulse
>
> <img src="images/media/image23.png" style="width:2.25833in;height:1.11875in" />Electrical activity on EKG

**Treatment**

> **CPR**
>
> **Epinephrine**
>
> **找可逆原因**
>
> **unshockable**

**<u>Tamponade EKG Association</u>**

> **Electrical alternans** can also be seen in tamponade
>
> **Alternating QRS amplitude** due to heart swinging in fluid

**Supraventricular Tachycardia and WPW**

<img src="images/media/image24.jpeg" style="width:4.63194in;height:1.48611in" />**<u>SVT</u>**

**Presentation**

> **Young person**
>
> Palpitations
>
> Syncope
>
> Tachycardia

**EKG**

> **Narrow QRS**

**Treatment**

> **1<sup>st</sup> step: <span class="mark">Vagal maneuvers</span>**

**Cold water to face**

**Carotid massage**

**Stimulate vagus nerve**

> **Next: <span class="mark">IV adenosine</span>**🡪blocks AV nodes🡪resets rhythm

If **<span class="mark">unstable</span>** (AMS, hypotension, ↓oxygen sat, ↓urine output, cold/cyanotic limbs)

> **IV access**
>
> **Sedation** + **<span class="mark">synchronized cardioversion</span>**

**Definitive Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Ablation</span>**

**<u>Wolff-Parkinson-White</u>**

**Pathophysiology**

> Accessory pathway bypasses AV node (low CO🡪low kidney灌注🡪HR↑🡪SVT)
>
> Can **trigger SVT**

**Presentation**

> Palpitations
>
> Syncope

**EKG**

> **<span class="mark">Delta wave</span>**
>
> P merges into QRS

**Most Accurate Test**

> **Electrophysiology study** (check how many times it goes through the accessory pathway)

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Procainamide</span>** （IA）↓ conduction through accessory pathway
>
> **Ablation**

**WPW + AF → 走旁路 → ventricular rate 会失控 → 用 procainamide，不要用 adenosine / β-blocker / CCB / digoxin**

**阻断房室结的药物会使所有电流通过旁路下传，导致心室率飙升诱发室颤**

| 类型 | ECG特点 | 首选治疗 | 关键禁忌/提示 |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| SVT（AVNRT/AVRT） | 规则、窄QRS | **① vagal ② adenosine** | 不稳定→电复律 |
| AF（普通） | 不规则不齐 | **β-blocker 或 diltiazem（**控率） | 抗凝看CHA₂DS₂-VASc |
| Atrial flutter | sawtooth | 同 AF |  |
| ❗WPW + AF | 不规则 + 宽QRS + 很快 | **procainamide / ibutilide** | 🚨 **禁 adenosine / BB / CCB / digoxin** |
| VT（有脉） | 规则、宽QRS | **amiodarone** | 不稳定→同步电复律 |
| Pulseless VT / VF | 无脉 | 🚨 defibrillation + CPR + epi |  |
| Torsades de pointes | polymorphic VT + QT长 | ⭐ **magnesium sulfate** | 纠正低K/低Mg |
| Bradycardia（症状性） | HR↓ | **atropine → pacing** |  |
| AV block（高阶） | PR延长/脱落 | pacing |  |
| Sinus tachycardia | 正常节律快 | 治原因（发热/疼痛/失血） | 不直接用抗心律药 |

> **Adenosine = 瞬间按停 AV 结（掐断“依赖AV结”的SVT）**
>
> **Atropine = 松开迷走刹车（让 SAN/AVN 更快、更通）**

**窄规则 → adenosine\
乱房颤 → β阻滞\
旁路房颤 → procainamide\
宽规则 → amiodarone\
扭转尖 → magnesium\
没脉 → 电击**

**【arrhythmia总结】**

**规则窄QRS SVT（AVNRT/AVRT）🡪vagal maneuvers, or adenosine**

**Atrial fibrillation🡪rate control (beta blocker or CCB)**

**<u>Electrolyte EKG Clues</u>**

**Hypocalcemia**

> <img src="images/media/image25.png" style="width:3.61875in;height:1.70347in" />Long **QT**

<img src="images/media/image26.png" style="width:1.49236in;height:1.38264in" />**Hypercalcemia**

> Short QT
>
> **acidosis**

**Hyperkalemia**

> **Peaked T waves**
>
> **acidosis**

**Hypokalemia**

> **U waves**
>
> **alkalosis**

What’s the underlying issue in **long QT syndrome?**

**Potassium trapped in cell🡪delayed repolarization**

**Valvular Disease**

**TTE🡪aortic valve; TEE🡪mitral valve, HOCM**

**<u>AORTIC STENOSIS</u>**

**Presentation**

> **Syncope**
>
> **<span class="mark">Angina</span>**
>
> Exertional dyspnea
>
> Chest pain

**Pulse**

> Pulsus **<span class="mark">parvus et tardus</span>** (weak/late, nothing getting out of valve, carotid pulse that is felt later than contraction)细迟脉dimished and delayed carotid pulses

**Best Initial Test**

> **Transthoracic echo/<span class="mark">TTE</span>**

**Most Accurate**

> **<span class="mark">Catheterization</span>** (see pressure in the ventricle🡪**high**)

**<u>Severe AS【背】</u>**

**<span class="mark">Valve area\<1.0cm<sup>2</sup></span>**

**Low pulse pressure: <span class="mark">systolic-diastolic\<25 mm Hg</span> （SV↓🡪脉压变窄）**

**Treatment**

**Asymptomatic**

> **<span class="mark">Diuretics</span>**

**Symptomatic**

> **<span class="mark">Valve replacement</span>**

**Most Common Cause**

> Aging

| **AS情况** | **处理** |
|:---|:---|
| 轻中度，无症状 | 观察 |
| **重度 + 症状<span class="mark">(呼吸困难、心绞痛、昏厥</span>)** | **AV replacement** |
| **重度 + <span class="mark">EF\<50%</span>** | **AV replacement** |

**<u>Heyde syndrome</u>: <span class="mark">老年人 + vWF 减少 + 镜检阴性出血</span> 🡪 瓣膜剪切 🡪 主动脉瓣狭窄 + 血管发育不良**

> **<span class="mark">钙化性主动脉瓣狭窄 (Calcific AS)</span>：高流速的血液通过狭窄的瓣膜时会产生巨大的剪切力 (Shear stress) 。**
>
> **<span class="mark">获得性 2A 型 vWD (Acquired vWS)</span>：这种剪切力会物理性地“粉碎”循环中的 高分子量 vWF 多聚体 。由于 vWF 负责血小板与内皮的粘附，多聚体缺失会导致初级止血功能受损 。**
>
> **<span class="mark">血管发育不良angiodysplasia出血</span>：患者胃肠道中原本存在的微小血管发育不良（在老年人中常见）在缺乏有效凝血支持的情况下开始出现顽固性出血 。**

**临床决策：通过瓣膜置换术 (AVR) 修复主动脉瓣通常能纠正 vWF 缺失并停止胃肠道出血 。**

**<u>Aortic Regurgitation</u>**

**Presentation**

> Head bobbing
>
> Quincke pulse甲床毛细血管波动（轻压甲床，甲床颜色一红一白地跳动🡪提示**收缩压↑ + 舒张压↓ → 脉压增宽，**导致末梢血流搏动特别明显）

**Best Initial Test**

> **Transthoracic echo**

**Most Accurate**

> **Catheterization** (see pressure in the ventricle🡪**low**)

**Treatment**

**Asymptomatic**

> **<span class="mark">ACE inhibitor</span>**🡪 afterload↓

**Symptomatic**

> **Valve replacement**

**Most Common Cause**

> **Aging**

**<u>Valve Replacement Types</u>**

**Bioprosthetic**

> No anticoagulation
>
> Replaced every **5–10 years**

**Mechanical**

> Long lasting
>
> Requires **anticoagulation**
>
> **INR goals**
>
> With **risk factors**: **2.5–3.5**
>
> Without **risk factors: 2–3**

**<u>Mitral Valve Prolapse</u>**

**Classic Finding**

> **Mid-systolic click**

**Presentation / Pathophysiology**

> More common in women / **estrogen-related** in notes
>
> Gets **louder when volume drops**
>
> Louder with **standing and Valsalva**
>
> Moves **closer to S1**

**Confirmation**

> Transesophageal echo/**<span class="mark">TEE</span>**

**<span class="mark">Symptomatic</span> Treatment**

> **Beta blockers** (more time to fill)

**Heart Failure and Cardiomyopathy**

**<u>Kussmaul</u>** = **吸气时 JVP 反升**，问题在于**右心“装不进去”**。正常吸气时静脉回流增加，右心应该能接住这股回流；如果右心室或心包太硬、太受限，血就“堵”在静脉端，于是 JVP 吸气时升高。

提示**右心充盈受限**；最有代表性的是 **缩窄性心包炎，也可见于restrictive cardiomyopathy、严重右心衰、右室梗死、重度三尖瓣反流/狭窄**\
**<u>pulsus paradoxus</u>** = **吸气时收缩压掉 \>10 mmHg**，问题在于**吸气时左心输出被明显压低**。吸气时右心充盈增加、室间隔左移，或心包压塞限制总心腔容积，导致左心充盈减少，所以吸气时收缩压明显下降。

最典型提示**心脏压塞**; 也常见于 **asthma、COPD** 等会明显增加胸腔压力摆动的情况。

**<u>Congestive Heart Failure</u>**

**Presentation**

> Fatigue
>
> Syncope
>
> Crackles
>
> Rales
>
> JVD
>
> Peripheral edema

**Labs**

> **BNP elevated** (released by ventricle when the fibers of heart are stretched🡪causes block of aldosterone🡪water leaves the body with the sodium)

**Imaging / Testing**

> **Echo** 🡪 check **ejection fraction**
>
> **Chest x-ray**:

Cardiomegaly

Pulmonary congestion

**Cephalization** **(胸片上肺上部血管异常明显，提示肺静脉压升高，最经典见于左心衰导致的肺静脉淤血)**

Fluid in lungs

**<u>Diastolic Dysfunction CHF</u>**

**EF**

> **Normal EF**

**Heart Sound**

> **S4**

**Treatment**

> **Spironolactone**
>
> **Diuretics**
>
> **Beta blocker**

**<u>Systolic Dysfunction CHF</u>**

**EF**

> Low EF

**Heart Sound**

> **S3**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Beta blocker</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Digoxin</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">ACE inhibitor</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Furosemide</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Spironolactone</span>**

**<span class="mark">First line</span>**

> **<span class="mark">Beta blocker</span>**

**<span class="mark">Second line</span>**

> **<span class="mark">Digoxin</span>**

**<u>High-Output Heart Failure</u>**

**Causes** (body demanding a lot of blood and heart is pumping hard)

> **Anemia**
>
> **Cancer**
>
> **Pregnancy**
>
> **AVM**
>
> **Beriberi**
>
> **Hyperthyroidism**

**EF**

> Often very high
>
> Around **70% or above**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 26%" />
<col style="width: 73%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>High-output heart failure</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Pathophysiology</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>↓ SVR 🡪 ↑ cardiac output &amp; ↑ venous return (preload↑)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Causes</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Morbid obesity (most common)</p>
<p><strong>Arteriovenous fistula</strong> (congenital or acquired)</p>
<p>Hyperthyroidism, severe anemia, advanced cirrhosis</p>
<p>Paget disease, <strong>thiamine deficiency</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Clinical presentation</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Hyperdynamic circulation (↑ Pulse pressure, warm extremities)</p>
<p>Peripheral &amp; pulmonary edema</p>
<p>Laterally displaced point of maximal impulse, systolic flow murmur</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Echocardiographic findings</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Dilated LV, RV &amp; inferior vena cava</p>
<p>Elevated resting cardiac index</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>Pulmonary edema</u>**

**CXR**

**早期血管压力升高**

**Pulmonary vascular redistribution** — **cephalization of vessels**

正常站立位时，下肺血管通常比上肺更粗；肺静脉压升高，上肺血管也变得很显眼，叫 **cephalization**，是**较早期的肺淤血表现**

**中期液体进入间质**

**Kerley B lines** — **horizontal lines** at lung periphery representing thickened interlobular septa (≥95% specificity)

液体先漏到**肺间质**，尤其进入小叶间隔，提示已有 **interstitial edema（间质性肺水肿），**常在肺底、肺外周看到

**Peribronchial cuffing** — edema of bronchial walls due to pulmonary vascular congestion

液体不仅进小叶间隔，也会积在 **支气管壁周围间质**，造成支气管壁水肿、增厚，**也是间质性肺水肿** 的表现之一

**晚期液体进入肺泡**

**Perihilar opacification** — "bat wing" or "butterfly" pattern

胸片中央、双肺门周围出现对称性阴影。当液体进一步进入**肺泡**，而肺门周围血流最丰富，所以液体和渗出常先/更明显集中在中央区域。**提示**从单纯间质水肿进展到 **alveolar edema（肺泡性水肿）**

**Airspace consolidation** — frank alveolar edema🡪严重低氧、呼吸困难

**伴随表现**

**Bilateral pleural effusions液体进入胸膜腔，漏出液**

**Management (mnemonic: <span class="mark">LMNOP</span>)** **= 改善氧合 + 降低肺毛细血管压力 + 减少前负荷/后负荷 + 处理病因**

> **Lasix （furosemide）减轻容量负荷**
>
> **Morphine**
>
> **Nitrates 扩v\>a，快速preload↓**
>
> **Oxygen/NPPV (CPAP, BiPAP）纠正低氧**
>
> **Position upright减少回心血量**

**<u>Dilated Cardiomyopathy</u>**

**Most Common Cause**

> **MI**

**Causes**

> **<span class="mark">MI</span>**
>
> **Heart block infections**
>
> **HIV**
>
> **Coxsackie**
>
> **Doxorubicin**
>
> **Alcohol**

**Most Accurate Test**

> **<span class="mark">MUGA scan</span>** –**special test for chemo** (check actual functioning of the ventricular)

MUGA scan 是核素心室造影，用来<u>**定量**评估**左心室射血分数**</u>，最经典用于监测蒽环类化疗药（如 **doxorubicin）的心脏毒性**。

**Echocardiographic findings🡪看心脏变大、泵力变差、返流和血栓**

Global LV hypokinesis左心室整体收缩减弱

LV and LA dilation

reduced LVEF

**functional MR**

**intracardiac thrombi**

**CMR findings**: 心脏MRI🡪**更精准看容积和是否有纤维化**

**Gold standard** for **biventricular volumes** and **systolic function**

**late gadolinium enhancement (LGE) in a mid-myocardial pattern** (particularly basal septum) indicates **fibrosis** and is a strong predictor of outcomes and sudden cardiac death risk

> 延迟钆增强呈**心肌中层强化**，尤其是**基底部室间隔**，提示心肌纤维化，是**预后差、猝死风险高** 的强预测因素

**Global longitudinal strain**看心肌纵向纤维在收缩时缩短了多少🡪**更早发现收缩功能开始变坏**

Reduced even **before LVEF decline**

predicts cardiovascular events beyond LVEF

**<u>HOCM</u>**

**Inheritance**

> Autosomal dominant

**Defect**

> Irregularly displaced myocardial fibers
>
> Septum hypertrophied
>
> Mitral leaflet contributes to outflow obstruction

**Diagnosis**

> Transesophageal echo/**TEE**

**Management**

> **Hydration**
>
> **<span class="mark">Beta blocker</span>** (heart more time to fill)
>
> **Avoid extreme exercise**
>
> **Pacemaker**
>
> **Septal surgery** if needed

**<u>Restrictive Cardiomyopathy</u>**

**Causes**

> **Amyloidosis**
>
> **Hemochromatosis**
>
> Sarcoidosis

**Type of Dysfunction**

> Diastolic

**Presentation**

> **<span class="mark">Kussmaul sign</span>**: JVD increases with **inspiration**右心充盈受限
>
> **正常生理**：吸气时，胸腔内产生负压，血液会被“吸”入右心房，因此颈静脉压力应该**下降**。
>
> **病理状态**：在**<span class="mark">缩窄性心包炎constrictive pericarditis</span>**，心包变得僵硬、增厚且失去弹性，像一个“硬壳”锁住了心脏。
>
> **吸气时的冲突**：吸气时胸腔负压增加，试图回流的血液增加，但由于右心室被僵硬的心包限制，无法扩张来接纳这些额外的血液。血液“堵”在了入口处，导致<span class="mark">颈静脉压力反而**升高**</span>。

**<span class="mark">吸气时颈静脉怒张反而加重（库斯莫尔征）= 右心室充盈受阻，首选诊断为缩窄性心包炎。</span>**

**Treatment**

> Treat **underlying cause**
>
> **Diuretics**

| **疾病关联 (Association)** | **前体蛋白 (Precursor)** | **临床特征 (Clinical Features)** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **原发性 (AL)** | **免疫球蛋白轻链 (Light chains)** | **<span class="mark">肾病综合征（蛋白尿）、巨舌</span>、皮肤瘀斑、心脏受累** |
| **老年性 (ATTR)** | **转甲状腺素蛋白 (TTR)** | **老年男性常见，心脏受累、<span class="mark">腕管综合征 (CTS)</span>** |
| **继发性 (AA)** | **血清淀粉样蛋白 A (SAA)** | **长期慢性炎症/感染相关 (如类风湿、TB)** |

> 心电图陷阱：虽然超声显示心室肥厚，但由于**淀粉样蛋白不导电**，ECG 往往表现为**低电压（Low voltage）**，这种“**<span class="mark">厚心壁+低电压</span>**”的矛盾是诊断的关键提示 。
>
> 确诊金标准：受累器官活检，在**刚果红染色（Congo red stain）**下观察到苹果绿双折射（Apple-green birefringence） 。
>
> 治疗：主要针对原发病。利尿剂可缓解症状，但需**谨慎使用以维持足够的心室充盈压**。

Cardio's Note: 记住“**<span class="mark">二高一低”：超声显示高度肥厚、心衰症状高度典型，但心电图电压低</span>**。如果还伴有蛋白尿或腕管综合征，直接锁定淀粉样变性！

**老妇受刺激，像心梗，冠脉却通——Takotsubo**

**Tamponade, Shock, and Pericardial Disease**

**<u>Cardiac Tamponade</u>**

**Causes**

> **Trauma**
>
> **MI**
>
> **Aortic dissection**

**Presentation**

> **<span class="mark">Beck triad</span>**

**Hypotension**

<img src="images/media/image27.png" style="width:4.10556in;height:1.78819in" />**distended neck veins/JVD**

**distant heart sounds**

> **<span class="mark">Pulsus paradoxus</span>: Drop** in systolic **BP \>10** mmHg with **inspiration**
>
> **Also Seen In**
>
> **COPD**
>
> **Asthma**
>
> **Lung sounds are normal**

**Most Accurate Test**

> **Echocardiogram** (look for **right heart collapse**, no blood inside)

**Treatment**

**If BP normal**

> **<span class="mark">Pericardiocentesis</span>**

**If BP low**

> <span class="mark">**Fluids** first</span>
>
> Then **pericardiocentesis**

**Hemodynamics**

> **Low PCWP** (everything is around the heart not inside)

**EKG**

> **Electrical alternans** (beat to beat variation in QRS amplitude due to the swinging of the heart in the blood-filled pericardium)

<table style="width:90%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 17%" />
<col style="width: 72%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>

<p>Cardiac tamponade</p>
</blockquote></th>

<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Etiology</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Blood in pericardial space (eg, left ventricular rupture, cardiac surgery)</p>
<p>Pericardial effusion (eg, malignancy, infection, uremia)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Clinical signs</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Beck triad</strong>: hypotension, JVD, ↓ heart sounds</p>
<p><strong>Pulsus paradoxus</strong>: &gt;10 mm Hg drop in SBP during inspiration</p>
</blockquote></td>

</blockquote></td>

<p>ECG: <strong>low-voltage QRS complex, electrical alternans</strong></p>
<p>Chest x-ray: <strong>enlarged cardiac silhouette [subacute]</strong>,* <strong>clear lungs</strong></p>

<p>Drainage via <strong><mark>pericardiocentesis or pericardial window</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>

</blockquote></td>

> <img src="images/media/image28.png" style="width:5.93422in;height:2.14412in" />

**Acute tamponate🡪右心先被压（本身压力低）， right atrial pressure↑🡪右心充盈受阻🡪回心血进不去🡪clear lungs + PCWP↑🡪心输出量CI↓🡪obstructive shock**

**With progress🡪all 4 chambers↑，equalize with percardial pressure**

高频对比

**Cardiac tamponade**

> JVD
>
> hypotension
>
> clear lungs
>
> no pulmonary edema
>
> equalized diastolic pressures

**Left-sided cardiogenic pulmonary edema**

> PCWP truly elevated due to backward failure
>
> pulmonary congestion
>
> crackles
>
> dyspnea
>
> edema in lungs

**<u>Cardiogenic Shock</u>**

**Most Common Cause**

> **MI**

**Hemodynamics**

> **↓CO**
>
> **↑HR, SVR, PCWP**

**<u>Obstructive shock</u>**

**CVP↑，CO↓**

**Prepulmonary (massive PE, tension pneumothorax)**🡪**PCWP↓**

**Postpulmonary (left heart, aorta)**🡪**PCWP↑**

**<u>Hypovolemic shock echo/hemodynamics:</u>**

> **small chambers**
>
> **hyperdynamic LV**
>
> **high EF**
>
> **low filling pressures**

**失血休克 = 心脏“没血可打” → 左室变小，但收缩更猛，EF 反而高**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 84%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>ACUTE PERICARDITIS</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Etiology</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Viral or idiopathic</strong></p>
<p>Autoimmune disease (eg, <strong><mark>SLE</mark></strong>)</p>
<p><strong><mark>Uremia</mark></strong> (acute or chronic kidney failure)</p>
<p><strong><mark>Post myocardial infarction</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p>Early: <strong><u>peri-infarction pericarditis</u> (&lt;4d, delayed reperfusion risk↑)</strong></p>
<p>Late: <strong><u>Dressler syndrome</u> (数周-数月)</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Clinical features &amp; diagnosis</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Pleuritic chest pain (↓ when sitting) ± fever</p>
<p>Pericardial <strong>friction rub</strong> (highly specific)</p>
<p><strong>ECG</strong>: <mark><strong>diffuse ST-segment elevation</strong> &amp; <strong>PR-segment depression</strong></mark></p>
<p><strong><mark>Echocardiography</mark></strong>: pericardial effusion, r/o other complications (free wall rupture)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Treatment</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>NSAIDs &amp; colchicine</mark></strong> for <strong>viral or idiopathic</strong> etiology</p>
<p>Variable for other etiologies</p>
<p><strong>Post MI should avoid NSAIDs</strong> for at least <strong>7 days</strong> (risk of free wall rupture)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<img src="images/media/image29.jpeg" style="width:6.52708in;height:5.49931in" />

**无论哪种心包炎，出现<span class="mark">新发胸痛</span>第一步：<span class="mark">Echo</span>🡪是否有大量积液导致心包填塞，是否有心肌破裂迹象**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 11%" />
<col style="width: 10%" />
<col style="width: 10%" />
<col style="width: 30%" />
<col style="width: 36%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Acute pericarditis</strong></p>
</blockquote></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>总称</strong></p>
</blockquote></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>任何时间</strong></p>
</blockquote></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>多种原因</strong></p>
</blockquote></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><u>Viral/idiopathic</u>:</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>NSAID</mark>（Ibuprofen，indomethacin,</strong></p>
<p><strong>high-dose aspirin) + <mark>colchicine</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Steroids if refractory</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Peri-infarction</strong></p>
<p><strong>pericarditis</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>MI后早期心包炎</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>1–4天</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>局部炎症（心肌透壁坏死直接累及邻近心包）🡪坐位减轻的胸痛；弥漫性 PR 段压低；超声示少量积液</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Supportive</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Acetaminophen for pain control</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>避免NSAID</mark> or <mark>steroid</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>（myocardial rupture risk）</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>PCIS</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>心脏损伤后</strong></p>
<p><strong>免疫性心包炎</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>数周–数月</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>自身免疫🡪发热、乏力；广泛心包/胸腔积液；炎症指标（CRP/ESR）升高🡪治疗重点：抗炎</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>NSAID（high dose aspirin）</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>±<mark>colchicine</mark> (减少复发)</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Steroids</mark> if refractory or renal insufficiency</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Dressler syndrome</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>MI后的PCIS</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>数周–数月</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>自身免疫</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>同上</strong></p>
<p><strong>避免/小心anticoagulation</strong></p>
<p><strong>（hemorrhagic pericardial effusion）</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**症状基本一样：**

**pleuritic chest pain, <span class="mark">深呼吸加重</span>，<span class="mark">lean forward缓解</span>，常向肩部放射can radiate posteriorly to the bilateral trapezius ridges (lower aspect of the bilateral scapulae)**

**pericardial friction rub**

**Auscultation at the left sternal border: triphasic pericardial friction rub (heard in atrial systole, ventricular systole, and early ventricular diastole). **

**Serum troponin may be slightly elevated**

**<span class="mark">diffuse ST elevation，PR depression</span>**

**🔑 一句话总结：Acute pericarditis 是总称；Peri-infarction pericarditis 是 MI 后 1–4 天的炎症；PCIS 是心脏损伤后数周的免疫性心包炎；Dressler syndrome 是 MI 引起的 PCIS。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 0%" />
<col style="width: 74%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>Post–cardiac injury syndrome</strong></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"></th>

<p>Causes</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Myocardial infarction</strong> (ie, Dressler syndrome)</p>
<p><strong>Cardiac surgery</strong> or trauma</p>
<p><strong>Percutaneous coronary intervention</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Clinical features</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Latent period of <strong>several weeks to months</strong></p>
<p><strong>Pleuritic chest pain, fever, leukocytosis</strong></p>
<p>Chest x-ray: <strong>pleural effusion</strong> ± <strong>enlarged cardiac silhouette</strong></p>
<p>Echocardiography: <strong>pericardial effusion</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Treatment</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><mark>NSAID</mark> (usually high-dose aspirin) ± <strong>colchicine</strong></p>
<p><mark>Corticosteroid</mark> in <strong>refractory</strong> disease</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>

<p>Prognosis</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Usually <strong>self-limited</strong> disease course</p>
<p>May cause <strong>chronic/recurrent</strong> disease leading to <strong>constrictive pericarditis</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**【Uremic pericarditis】acute or chronic renal failure and BUN \>60 mg/dL**

**classic ECG findings of diffuse ST-segment elevation and PR-segment depression are <span class="mark">typically absent</span> (inflammation from uremic pericarditis does not involve the myocardium)**

**Treatment: <span class="mark">dialysis</span>；**

**anticoagulation is contraindicated (elevated bleeding risk eg, uremia-induced platelet dysfunction).**

**【acute pericarditis due to SLE】**

**most common cardiac manifestation of SLE, occurs in active disease (eg, joint pain, fatigue, malar rash, anemia, thrombocytopenia), pericardial effusions are often observed but small**

**Treatment:**

**1<sup>st</sup> line: <span class="mark">NSAIDs (eg, ibuprofen)</span>**

**Corticosteroids (eg, <span class="mark">prednisone</span>): contraindication to NSAIDs (eg, renal insufficiency), do not respond to NSAIDs.**

**<u>Constrictive Pericarditis</u>**

**Difference from Restrictive Cardiomyopathy**

> Constrictive pericarditis = diseased, scarred pericardium
>
> Restrictive cardiomyopathy = infiltrative myocardial disease

**constrictive=心包问题（外面硬壳），不是restrictive=心肌问题（里面变硬）**

<img src="images/media/image30.png" style="width:4.88889in;height:1.15718in" />

**Constrictive pericarditis 是心包限制导致的舒张障碍（有Kussmaul、pericardial knock、呼吸依赖）**

**restrictive cardiomyopathy 是心肌本身变硬（常见于amyloidosis），BNP更高且不受呼吸影响明显。**

**Pathophysiology**

> Pericardial **scarring and calcification**
>
> Prevents heart from expanding normally
>
> **Idiopathic**, or triggered by a **viral infection**

**Presentation**

> Edema
>
> JVD
>
> Exertional dyspnea
>
> Ascites
>
> **Kussmaul-type** findings
>
> **Pericardial knock** (diastolic knocking sound just after the second heart sound)

**Tests**

> **Chest x-ray**: **calcification**
>
> **Echo / CT / MRI**: **thickened pericardium**
>
> Ventricular biopsy normal

**Treatment**

> **Surgical pericardiectomy**

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20%" />
<col style="width: 79%" />

<tr>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Etiology</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Recurrent idiopathic or viral pericarditis</strong></p>
<p><strong>Cardiac surgery</strong> or <strong>radiation</strong> therapy</p>
<p><strong><mark>Tuberculous pericarditis</mark></strong> (endemic areas)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Clinical presentation</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Fatigue, dyspnea on exertion</p>
<p>Peripheral edema, ascites, hepatic congestion</p>
<p>Pericardial knock in early diastole</p>
<p>Elevated JVP with <strong>Kussmaul sign</strong>*</p>
<p><strong>Prominent y descent</strong> of JVP waveform</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Diagnostic findings</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Chest x-ray: <strong>pericardial calcification</strong></p>
<p>Cardiac CT scan/MRI: pericardial thickening &amp; calcification</p>
<p>Echocardiography: <mark><strong>biatrial enlargement</strong>, normal ventricular wall thickness &amp; cavity size</mark>, abnormal septal motion during respiration</p>
<p>主要问题是 <strong>心室舒张充盈受限🡪</strong>血液回到心脏，<strong>心室装不进去</strong>🡪心房必须在更高压力下把血“往里送”🡪久而久之<strong>左右心房扩大</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">*Absence of the expected fall in JVP during inspiration. JVP = jugular venous pulse.</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Hematogenous or direct intrathoracic spread</p>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>ECG: tachycardia, <strong>diffuse ST-segment elevation</strong>, ± <strong>low-voltage QRS complexes</strong></p>
<p>CXR: <strong>enlarged cardiac silhouette &amp; clear lung fields</strong></p>
<p>Echocardiography: pericardial effusion</p>
<p>Cytology: turbid fluid with ↑ WBCs (neutrophil predominant), ↑ protein, ↓ glucose</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;">Treatment</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Intravenous antibiotics</mark> + urgent <mark>pericardial drainage</mark> (诊断🡪Gram stain, culture+治疗)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<img src="images/media/image31.png" style="width:3.95694in;height:2.52569in" />

**<u>HYPERTENSION management</u>**

**Elevated BP**

> **120–129 / \<80**
>
> **<span class="mark">生活方式干预</span>**

**Stage 1 HTN**

> **130–139 或 80–89**
>
> **生活方式**
>
> **<span class="mark">若有 ASCVD/CKD/DM 或 10 年 ASCVD 风险高</span> → <span class="mark">加药</span>**

**Stage 2 HTN**

> **≥140 或 ≥90**
>
> **生活方式 + 药物**
>
> <img src="images/media/image32.png" style="width:1.62847in;height:1.31875in" />**<span class="mark">若 ≥20/10 above goal → 2 药起始</span>**

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 26%" />

</blockquote></td>

<p><strong>based on ventricular ejection fraction</strong></p></td>

<colgroup>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>

</blockquote></td>

<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Osteoporosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Thiazide diuretic</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Migraine</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>β Blocker, CCB</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Calcium kidney stones</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Thiazide diuretic</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<u>**Calcium channel blocker** (CCB)</u>

dihydropyridines CCB （amlodipine）🡪**dilation of precapillary vessels** (arteriolar dilation)🡪<span class="mark">**peripheral edema**,</span> **headache, flushing, and lightheadedness**.

ACEi/ARB🡪**post-capillary venodilation**🡪help normalize ↑capillary hydrostatic pressure caused by CCB

**<span class="mark">CCB +ACE inhibitor</span>** 🡪 **<span class="mark">lower risk of CCB-associated peripheral edema</span>**

**CCB引起的外周水肿源于毛细血管静水压增高，首选联合使用CCB+ ACEI 或 ARB 扩张小静脉🡪缓解外周水肿症状并强化降压效果**

**<span class="mark">β-blocker</span>**

**优先考虑用于：**

**CAD / angina / prior MI**

**HFrEF**

**AF rate control**

**副作用：**

Bradyarrhythmias

Generalized fatigue

Sexual dysfunction

↑airway resistance

Worsening decompensated HF

**Losartan (ARB)，atrovastatin 促尿酸排泄**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20%" />
<col style="width: 58%" />
<col style="width: 20%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="3" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Lifestyle interventions for hypertension</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Modification</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Recommended plan</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Approximate ↓</strong></p>
<p><strong>systolic BP (mm Hg)</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>DASH diet</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">Diet high in fruits &amp; vegetables &amp; low in saturated &amp; total fats</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">11</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Weight loss</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">Reduction of BMI to &lt;25 kg/m<sup>2</sup></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">6 per 10-kg loss</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Aerobic exercise</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">30 minutes/day for 5+ days/week</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">7</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Dietary sodium</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">&lt;1.5-2.3 g/day (response varies)</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">5-8</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Alcohol limitation</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">≤2 drinks/day in men, ≤1 drink/day in women</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">5</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="3" style="text-align: left;"><strong>DASH</strong> = <strong>D</strong>ietary <strong>A</strong>pproaches to <strong>S</strong>top <strong>H</strong>ypertension. 强调高水果、蔬菜、豆类和低脂乳制品，降低饱和脂肪和总脂肪摄入。其综合营养成分对血管内皮和血压调节有显著益处。</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**戒烟**不能显著降压，但它是预防中风和心肌梗死等**终点事件**最有效的方法之一，必须强烈推荐

新发高血压初步评估：血糖、血脂和肾功（电解质+尿常规）、心电图，识别潜在的靶器官损害和糖尿病、血脂异常等合并症

<table style="width:71%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20%" />

年轻人，viral infection🡪myocarditis🡪decompensated heart failure🡪dilated cardiomyopathy

<table style="width:90%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 13%" />
<col style="width: 76%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">Viral myocarditis</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Clinical presentation</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Commonly <strong>asymptomatic</strong> &amp; resolves without detection</p>
<p>Heart failure that may progress to DCM*</p>
<p><strong>Chest pain, ventricular arrhythmia</strong> with risk of <strong>SCD</strong></p>
<p> Relatively <strong>young adults</strong> usually affected (eg, age &lt;55)</p>
<p>± <strong>Viral prodrome</strong> (eg, fever, malaise, myalgia)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Diagnosis</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>ECG: nonspecific</strong> findings</p>
<p>Laboratory: mild to moderate <strong>serum troponin elevation</strong></p>
<p><strong>Echocardiography</strong>: <strong>4-chamber dilation with diffuse hypokinesis</strong></p>
<p>Cardiac <strong>MRI: epicardial or midwall enhancement</strong></p>
<p><strong>Biopsy</strong>: <strong>lymphocytic infiltration</strong>, viral DNA or RNA**</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Treatment</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Supportive care</mark></strong> to allow time for recovery</p>
<p><strong><mark>HFrEF medications</mark> (eg, diuretic, ACE inhibitor, beta blocker)</strong></p>
<p>Temporary ventricular assist device, if needed</p>
<p><strong>Heart transplant</strong> if no recovery</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p>*Most common symptomatic presentation.</p>
<p>**Endomyocardial biopsy is rarely required for diagnosis.</p>
<p>DCM = dilated cardiomyopathy; HFrEF = heart failure with reduced ejection fraction; SCD = sudden cardiac death.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p>*Some etiologies may cause persistent contractile dysfunction that can progress to dilated cardiomyopathy.</p>
<p>**Most common cause.</p>
<p>RMSF = Rocky Mountain spotted fever; SLE = systemic lupus erythematosus.</p></td>

**Infective Endocarditis and Vascular Disease**

**<u><span class="mark">Acute</span> Bacterial Endocarditis</u>**

**Most Common Organism / Valve**

> **Staph aureus**
>
> **Tricuspid valve** in **<span class="mark">healthy</span> valve** setting

**Best Initial**

> **TEE + blood cultures**

**Empiric Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">IV vancomycin + gentamicin</span>**

Vancomycin 破坏细菌细胞壁，使 gentamicin 能进入细胞发挥抑制蛋白合成的作用，从而产生协同杀菌效应，常用于 enterococcal endocarditis。

用于**Enterococcus，endocarditis，need synergy。**

**If Culture Shows Strep gallolyticus or Clostridium**

> **Colonoscopy**

**Endocarditis Prophylaxis with penicillin**

For **strep viridans / mutans** in patients with:

> **Prior endocarditis**
>
> **Congenital heart disease**
>
> High-risk procedures such as **dental, respiratory, GI, skin procedures** per these notes

**<u><span class="mark">Subacute</span> Bacterial Endocarditis</u>**

**Most Common Organism / Valve**

> **Strep viridans or mutans**
>
> **Damaged** **<span class="mark">mitral</span>** valve

<table style="width:96%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 21%" />
<col style="width: 74%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Prevention</strong> of <strong>infective endocarditis</strong> with <strong><mark>antimicrobial prophylaxis</mark></strong>*</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p>High-risk procedures</p>
<p>(Prophylaxis needed)</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Gingival/apical <strong>tooth manipulation</strong> (<mark>amoxicillin</mark>)</p>
<p><strong><mark>Respiratory mucosa</mark></strong> incision (amoxicillin)</p>
<p>Surgery on <strong>infected skin or muscle</strong> (<mark>vancomycin</mark>)</p>
<p><strong>GI or GU</strong> procedure in setting of <strong>active infection</strong> (ampicillin)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p>Low-risk procedures</p>
<p>(No prophylaxis)</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>GI or GU</strong> endoscopy/procedure in <strong>absence of infection</strong></p>
<p>Most <strong>vaginal/caesarian deliveries</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">*Indicated for high-risk patients (eg, prosthetic heart valve, previous infective endocarditis, certain congenital cyanotic heart diseases).</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

机械瓣是 IE 高危人群，但 **routine screening colonoscopy** 不属于需要感染性心内膜炎预防性抗生素的操作，因此不需要抗生素预防。

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Local (cardiac)</strong></td>

<p>Pericarditis</p>

</blockquote></td>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Septic embolism脑卒中（败血性栓塞）</p>
<p>Metastatic abscess</p>

<p>Organ infarction脾肾梗死</p>

**<u>Common <span class="mark">surgical</span> indications in infectious endocarditis</u>**

> **<span class="mark">Acute heart failure</span> (eg, AR/MR)**
>
> **Extension of infection (eg, abscess, fistula, heart block)**
>
> **Difficult-to-eradicate organism (eg, fungus, multidrug-resistant pathogen)**
>
> **Persistent bacteremia on antibiotics**
>
> **Very high risk of embolism: large vegetation (\>1cm)/persistent septic emboli**

**感染性心内膜炎患者出现新发杂音和急性心衰体征，提示急性瓣膜功能不全，应立即行<span class="mark">超声心动</span>图评估手术指征。**

**1️⃣ 题干关键词抓考点**

> **基础病：** 明确诊断为**急性细菌性心内膜炎**。
>
> **突发呼吸困难 + 肺部湿啰音 (Crackles)：** 提示急性左心衰竭/肺水肿。
>
> **心脏杂音的演变（关键！）：**

**入院时：** 心音正常，无杂音。

**目前：** 出现**新发的早期舒张期杂音 (New early diastolic murmur)**。这在 IE 背景下是**主动脉瓣关闭不全 (AR)** 的典型体征。

**S3 心音：** 提示左心室容量负荷过重，进一步证实心衰。

> **低血压 (100/50 mmHg)：** 提示心输出量受损，可能处于心源性休克的早期。

**IE 并发症的“ECG 警报”**

| 看到这个体征 | 想到这个并发症 | 后续动作 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 新发 PR 间期延长 | **主动脉瓣周脓肿 (Perivalvular Abscess)** | **<span class="mark">TEE</span>** + 手术咨询 |
| 突发呼吸困难 + 新发杂音 | **急性瓣膜毁损/急性心衰** | Echo + 手术咨询 |
| 新发神经系统缺失/偏瘫 | **脓毒性栓塞 (Septic Emboli)** | 头部 MRI + 评估瓣膜 |
| 腰痛 + 发热 | **椎体骨髓炎 (Vertebral Osteomyelitis)** | 脊柱 MRI |

**💡 考场秒杀技巧**

> **IE + New Murmur = Echo (TEE is better).**
>
> **IE + New Heart Block = Abscess (Look for Perivalvular abscess).**
>
> **IE + Acute SOB + Crackles = Acute Valve Destruction (Emergency Surgery may be needed).**

| **受累瓣膜** | **并发症倾向** | **对传导系统的影响** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **主动脉瓣 (Aortic)** | **更易形成<span class="mark">瓣周脓肿</span>** | **极易导致<span class="mark">新发传导阻滞 (AV Block)</span>**。 |
| **二尖瓣 (Mitral)** | 更易导致<span class="mark">腱索断裂🡪急性心衰</span> | 较少直接引起传导阻滞（除非脓肿极大）。 |

**<u>感染性心内膜炎的手术指征</u>**

| **指征** | **临床表现 / 证据** |
|:---|:---|
| **急性心力衰竭** | **由于瓣膜关闭不全, 如<span class="mark">新发 AR/MR🡪肺水肿</span>。** |
| **感染控制失败** | 抗生素治疗下持续发热、血培养持续阳性。 |
| **局部并发症** | <span class="mark">**瓣周脓肿 (Perivalvular abscess)**🡪新发传导阻滞</span>。 |
| **高栓塞风险** | 赘生物体积过大（通常\>10 mm）或反复发生栓塞。 |
| **特殊致病菌** | 如真菌（Fungal IE）或耐药性极强的细菌。 |

**<u>Abdominal Aortic Aneurysm</u>**

**Risk Factors**

> **Hypertension**
>
> **Atherosclerosis/plaques**
>
> **Smoking**

**Presentation**

> Often **asymptomatic**
>
> **Pulsatile abdominal mass**
>
> **Bruit**

**Diagnosis**

> **<span class="mark">Focused abdominal ultrasound</span>**

**After Ultrasound, if stable**

**<span class="mark">CT</span>** to measure **size**

| **怀疑AAA** | **下一步🡪先确诊，再手术！** |
|:---|:---|
| **hemodynamically stable + suspected AAA** | **<span class="mark">CT abdomen</span>** |
| **unstable + known AAA** | **直接 <span class="mark">emergency repair</span>** |
| **unstable + suspected AAA but no known history** | **<span class="mark">focused bedside abdominal ultrasound</span>** |

**若没确诊：稳定🡪CT, 不稳定🡪床旁超声**

<table style="width:69%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20%" />
<col style="width: 48%" />
</colgroup>

<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">Screening: abdominal aortic aneurysm</th>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Men</p>
<p>Age 65-75</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Risk factor indication</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Any smoking history</p>

<p><strong>1-time</strong> <strong><mark>abdominal duplex ultrasonography</mark></strong></p>

</tbody>
</table>

**Treatment**

> **Surgery if \>5 cm** or **rapidly growing**

**男性：5.5 cm**

**女性：5.0 cm**

**快速增大：\>0.5 cm/6个月**

**Open surgical repair**

**or endovascular aneurysm repair**
